name:W‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçm‚Äçm‚Äçu‚Äçz‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçi
info:Deluxe King Room
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:68 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted July 4, 2021
msg:I saw the new Sheraton Panyu on the Internet, so I came to visit the store. As an amateur hotel enthusiast, share your personal experience and feelings. As the executive lounge was temporarily closed due to the epidemic, we chose a deluxe double room for one night, including a single breakfast.

Welcome/gate: Driving the door to the guests is the basic requirement of a five-star hotel, and Sheraton has done it.

Front desk: Check-in is unambiguous, clean and tidy, the time is within 5 minutes, and I am very familiar with the process. Requests for late smoking rooms, high floors, and late check-outs all met my needs. At the same time, I also informed me of the dining floor and elevator location tomorrow morning. This is the detail. The hall does not have a strong aroma, maybe because of wearing a mask, there is no fine product.

Room: The room is arranged on the 30th floor. The elevator will automatically identify the floor by swiping the card. One card is one floor, and the security is in place. The room layout is comfortable, the activity space is spacious, the lighting is basically divided into bright and soft, which is my favorite brightness. The air conditioner is set to a maximum wind speed of 22 degrees, and the room temperature can be maintained at approximately 23.5 degrees. The washing and care brand in Sheraton is undoubtedly the Le Grain Bain brand, with a strong background, and I regret not asking for more.

Breakfast: In the case of possible epidemics, a semi-self-service format is adopted. Basically, for hot food, the waiter will place an order for the residents alone, and the cold salad bake is maintained in self-service mode. The ice latte I requested can also be prepared for me. There are about 5 waiters in the restaurant. The service and quality are excellent. I score 10 points individually.

Location: Behind the hotel is a variety of cafes, convenience stores and gourmet food, just 1 minute walk from the door. There are also several large shopping malls in the surrounding area and it is convenient to take a taxi.

bonus: 
1) The water pressure in the room is superb, the biggest I have seen in any five-star hotel in the past ten or twenty years.
2) There is no need to heat up and wait for the hot water, just open it.
3) There are JBL Bluetooth alarm clock speakers in the room.
4) Features of hair dryer, retractable power cord.

Disadvantages:
1) The soundproofing of the room is not ideal, the noise in the corridor is easy to be introduced into the room, and the sound of water pressure in the next room penetrates, which is enough to affect sleep. Since it is a structural and decoration problem, although it is difficult to rectify, you can consider preparing disposable earplugs in the guest room to give light sleepers a touch of warmth.
2) The vanity mirror is not light enough. If the small mirror has a light, it will be a bonus.
3) There are no bath salts and toiletries in the bathtub.
4) The texture of the bathrobe is good, but for the tenants over 180 kg, it is lonely to wear, I really can't accept it.

Summary: If I go to Panyu, I will choose Sheraton, but I really hope that my self-esteem will not be stimulated by the bathrobe.
